< text>
Easy to find on highway 18 ample parking, very handicap friendly. Orders to go or dinning room open.  Wow big upgrade since the remodel 2020 looks very clean and nice. The restaurant seems more lit up with beautiful mural seating benches, Love the blue lighting around the bar entrance. Manuel are server was awesome & lots patience, We were a party of seven, it's not easy taking four very young children out to eat, Manuel got all the food orders perfect and it tasted phenomenal.  We ordered... quesadillas with french fries, quesadillas with beans and rice, chile rellenos, carne asada plates, combo plates with enchiladas & tamales, even the sample platter, everything was hot and fresh tasted wonderful.</text>

<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
Adelitas Mexican food restaurant in Lucerne Valley California is delicious! For the most delicious Mexican food try Adelitas when your nearby.
After spending a fun afternoon of driving exciting quad atv's at "Happy Trails ATV Rentals" in Lucerne Valley-Ben Stone the owner recommended
Adelitas for mexican food-it was a great suggestion!
The service and staff at Adelitas Mexican Restaurant are very helpful,first rate and they always make suggestions from their extensive menu.
Their menu features traditional Mexican dishes that are really great and they also feature a very extensive Mexican fish dish menus that is excellent! They have seafood tacos,enchiladas,burritos,salads and appetizers galore!
There portions are generous and prices
are very fair for all that you get at Adelitas.
Family,kids and senior friendly,plenty of parking and convenient to other shops and store's .
This was a great family experiance at Adelitas Mexican Restaurant Lucerne Valley California!<//Text>

< Review>
A local refered me to Adelitas which is in my mind the beat way to hear about a restaurant. It was a quiet sunday night and only a few other guests were having dinner. A few guests were dropping by to pick up orders. The salsa is chunky and spicy. The chips are nice and salty. The carne asada was tasty, especially with lime added. Portions were generous and filling. Fried tacos were good and crunchy with fresh toppings and the rice was perfect.
The server was very nice and checked on me a few times. She had a smile the whole time.
I tried the fish tacos (Not pictured) the night before and they were good too. I will be dropping in again on my next visit.<//Review>

<date>1551152373435<//date><rating>1< /rating>< Review>
My husband and i stopped at this Adelitas Restaurant on our way back home from Big Bear Lake. We are an older couple so we don't eat very much. We just wanted a quick bite so we just ordered one small cup of soup and only one burrito that we were  going to share. The restaurant wasn't busy at all at the time, only a couple of other people were  there. We ordered and waited, a few more people come in and their order is taken. They bring us our one cup of soup and bring food to the other folks that came after us. More people come in and their order is taken. Before we know it everyone that is sitting that all came after us all had food on their table. And we are still waiting for our ONE burrito that my husband and I were going to share. Not six burritos just ONE. My husband asked the waitress why we were not being served. She said they just finished making it let me go get it. My husband said "well have they made our order yet"? The waitress saids I was just going to walk over there  to get it. Do you still want  it? With  no apologies to say so sorry for the inconvenience or for taking so long, I'll bring it right away. Nothing of the sort,  Just sarcastically asked us if we still wanted our ONE burrito. My husband and I were so upset, he told the waitress that we didn't want our order and we stood up. My husband asked for the bill but they did not charge us for 2 glasses of water and a small cup of soup. Horrible horrible  service.  I absolutely do not recommend this so called Adelitas Restaurant. If anyone is craving Mexican food you're better of looking elsewhere. A true Mexican restaurant offers extraordinary service to all their customers so as to feel all the comforts of home away from home. And this Adelitas Restaurant makes you feel none of that. What a disgrace to the proprietors of this so called Restaurant. Do not eat here worse service ever. Mc Donalds offers friendlier and promt service and their food is not bad at all.</Review>

<Date>1621150382249</Date><Gmap_id>0x8096f2622704252d:0xbb13750ec772c57c</Gmap_id>< text>
Wow! What a mind blowing 360 views of all of Yosemite. A must sight to visit but come prepared as it gets very windy, cold and dark real quick. Bring a strong headlight (don't rely on phones flash), snacks, water and patience. This place you have to go all the way to the top. The twilight hour is so beautiful here.

Most come here for a quick 2 min phone selfie and leave. What a waste of time! You need to sit here and take it all in, especially during sunset. This view might be one of the best I've seen in a long time. If you are a photographer bring your best long telephoto lens here. You'll be in here for hours like I was!

Be warned the hike is steep for quiet a long time and rough. It took some time to get to the top (est maybe 45 mins or more). I had some pretty sore feet after.< /text>
<username>Sevan</username>< Pictures>

Sentinel Dome is a loop trail but it was a little hard to find the back side. We started our hike to Taft Point. Taft is cool because you can literally look down the side of the cliff. It was nerve wrecking but a great experience. You have to walk back towards the parking lot to find the back side of Sentinel Dome. Mid way you will have a choice to pick left or right on the trail. They both lead the same way but if you turn left be prepared for some obstacles. It is at the side of the mountain. You‚Äôll get some great pictures but be prepared to climb over a few fallen trees and a pretty steep hike on a minor narrow trail. Went in September so the creeks and waterfalls were dry. The views when you finally get at the top of Sentinel were amazing. You get a 360 view of everything including Half Dome. The hike back to the parking lot was easier because it‚Äôs mostly down hill. The park itself is nice enough. However, bring a can or two of raid. It is like a giant ant hill, and that is not an exaggeration. Just make sure you dont leave a purse or cell phone behind or it'll seriously be gone in seconds.</Text>

< Review>
Absolutely beautiful park!! We chose this park based off its location. It is a middle point between Riverside, Rialto, Hemet, Covina and L.A. so it was the perfect place for my baby's first birthday party. There was PLENTY to do for all ages. Everyone commented on how beautiful and clean the park was. I enjoyed how flat the park is, it made it easy to find our party. There is a ton of grass space, which we used to rent umbrella tables and chairs. There were multiple birthday parties going on at the same time, however, we each had our own privacy. Quiet, peaceful, clean, easy to find... great park, will definitely be back!!!< /Review>

<userid>114446183803129412321<//userid>< Review>
The Nuui Cunni Center is an inspiring place to visit ~ not to mention the  great Potluck Lunches or Indian Tacos! And they have regular lessons on Arts & Crafts projects ~ like Gourd Art and Basket Weaving. Take your camera out back to see the garden and sculptures or walk down the dirt road toward the lake for some nice photogenic views of Lake Isabella, known locally as "Big Blue".</Review>

** Review based on Outside Dinning **

overall i do not have good experience with outside dinning at this location.  But it won' t be fair to give them "" 2 "" stars, because of the pandemic.  The food is still decent; just the surrounding is horrible.

Firstly, you have to make reservation on Yelp; i guess you can't just walk-in and wait for available table.  Once you have checked in at your time slot; staff will walk you to your table; and explained to you, no cash is accepted.  Then,  "waiting" is part of package.

the server is way too busy "travelling" between "kitchen" & serve.  some dishes were cold by the time gets to our table.

next time i would rather just "pick up" the food, instead dine at the ourdoor seating.</text>

< review>
Haven't been back in almost a year and the quality and customer service are still as top notch as I remember! Very impressed with how they're handling the new guidelines we all have to follow now. The paper on the table with dinning instructions was easy to follow and neat to use. The food was to die for, everything we ordered came in a timely fashion and all the necessary sauces/condiments were provided either beforehand at the table or arrived quickly at special request. The dumplings were delicious and came in large portions which are great for person partys. The only downsides I can think of is you have to make a reservation though Yelp since they no longer allow walk ups, but even that is quick and easy, and that it is a pricey meal. However, I do believe the quality of the food makes up for that.<//review>

< rating>

<Text>This place has a special place in my foodie heart because it's technically my first Michelin-rated restaurant and I got to share it with my close friends that have never had dim sum before. When I first told them about it and that it was at the Del Amo Mall, they looked at me with an odd look, but trusted my judgement and are now hooked on dim sum. What I like about this place is that you're able to get some high quality dim sum without having to break the bank. It's a little bit of wait, but it's affordable and delicious! I recommend making reservations or using the Yelp app to secure your place in line.

They are known for their soup dumplings (Xiao Long Bao), but everything else is also done very well too. If you never had dim sum before, I recommend getting a variety of dumplings including wontons in spicy sauce, pot stickers, steamed buns, and their soup dumplings of course. It's easy to share and you'll figure out what you will like best. Dim sum is kind of like the Asian version of tapas, but is geared towards morning/afternoon and is usually accompanied with hot tea. Hope you like this place as much as I do!< /Text>< Pictures>

< text>
Hidden gem inside a mall. If you go during dinner time there is a wait we were quoted a 45-65 min wait but actual time was about 35. You check in to get your name on the list and you give your phone number. You receive one text letting you know your in the system and the second text they send you check in get a menu and are seated within 10ish minutes. Even though there was a wait you can tell that they have a system down to move people along.< /text>

You will never see Chinese food at the mall the same ever again after eating here.

There are no heat lamps, chaffing trays, or a worker passing out free samples here. Din Tai Fung as a corporate chain now brings to the mall gourmet fine dining delicacies at fine dining prices to boot.

Famous are the juicy pork/soup dumplings that have claimed fame. Xie Long Bao is what we are talking about and Din Tai Fung does it the best in the market right now at an astonishing pace with teams of workers in behind a fishbowl. Of course, there are many other very tasty items on the menu also. Actually, this location like all others carries the same menu and consistency of quality and taste reign the land.

You really can't go wrong with almost all their dumpling selections, but I do tend to stay away from the seafood. Pair your meal with some noodles and string beans and you'll be satisfied.

Unfortunately, the wait times at this popular location is staggering. Expect a possible one hour wait on weekends and maybe more during certain popular hours. Also, if you aren't already aware, this is fine dining even though it is at the mall. Do expect a $30 ticket for each person if you're visiting casually, and $40 per person if you're hungry.< /review>

<review>Pandemic UPDATE: 9-1-20 Order curbside pickup or, starting today, they have a tent in the parking lot on the west (Hawthorne) side of the mall to dine in (see pics). Curbside pickup is the small white tent next to the dine-in tent. Place your order directly on the restaurant website since the other services take part of the restaurant's money. End Update.
Best Dim Sum in the south Bay. Arrive before you are hungry and plan on a minimum of 30-45 min wait. Can be up to 2 hours.

They will text when your table is ready so just wait in the que for the hostess in the middle. Return to the podium on the right when you get your page. Expect 10-15 min more of a wait when you return.

Hot Tip: grab an open chair at the full service bar if one is available. No wait list, just stand-up for an opening.< /review>< name>

<name>Mimi Lawrence<//name>< Gmap_id>
0x80dd4b2bbcf466fb:0x5b772d325bf8610e<//Gmap_id>
<Rating>5<//Rating><time>1568044173502</time><text>Ding Tai Feng is really for carb lovers, almost everything here is carbs! And that's why we never eat at any Ding Tai Feng restaurants because of gluten sensitivities and I am on low carb very often. Hubby really wanted to try this location at Del Amo in Torrance so I went along with him just this time!

We came in for a late lunch, had a couple drinks at the full bar while waiting for sister and her bf. The Hendrick's soda water and lime was a bit weak, but hubby's Grey Goose dry martini was very yummy. Menu was huge with almost all Chinese carbs items like dumplings, buns, dry noodles, wontons, noodle soups, fried rice, pot stickers, shao mai and more. They even had sweet dumplings as desserts. They do have limited vegetarian, vegan and gluten free items but they are just veggies and some rice items so they are supposed to be naturally gluten free?

After our waitress' detailed introduction of the menus, we decided on a few orders of their famous juicy kurobuta pork dumpling / xiao long bao, cod fish dumplings, kimchi & pork dumplings, shrimp & kurobuta pork pot stickers, spicy chicken wonton, saut√©ed mustard greens with shredded ginger, braised beef soup, chicken wonton soup, shrimp fried rice and chocolate & mochi XLB. The food was really delicious without MSG and not greasy at all. Everybody loved xiao long bao so we got more orders of just those. The other dumplings were yummy but not nearly as good as juicy pork XLB. Shrimp fried rice was the best I've ever had. I think it's better to just order XLB with soup, veggies and fried rice. That way you can have a more balanced meal than a whole bunch of different dumplings in my opinion. We had San Pellegrino and a few more Grey Goose martinis as beverages.

The service was top notch which was what we expected from an upscale Chinese restaurant. If you love dumplings you should really try Ding Tai Feng and you will enjoy it very much. For me it's a once in a long time thing cause I am still having headaches from all the gluten I ignored for this meal!</text></record>

<Rating>5< /Rating><Text>I've eaten at three or four DTF locations at least, both in and out of California.  The Santa Anita Mall and Torrance locations are my local haunts.   In each location the food is always exceptional.  The staff are well-trained and always are pleasant and efficient.   The management do a fine job keeping service and food quality to high standards.

When you order try to balance your meal with one of the lighter dishes at the front of the menu.  And order a green (they're great).  The soups are all quite good, and the dumplings ... well that's why one goes.  The xiao lin bao and spicy shrimp abd pork dumplings are musts if it's your first time.

This is a very successful chain and they are unfailingly busy.  You might have to wait if you try to dine at peak times.< /Text>< pics>

<Date>1531839310570</Date><rating>4<//rating><Text>We came here on a super busy day (the weekend before Christmas), so the mall was very crowded, but we were seated within 10 minutes. We spent that time looking through the window in the front of the restaurant where you can watch the staff prepare fresh dumplings! It's definitely a little mesmerizing since they have a little dumpling assembly line going on, so it's nice to pass the time.

After we got seated, our server Jedi (FYI, it's not pronounced the Star Wars way) walked us through the menu and ordering process since we haven't been there before. It's basically a list of all the menu items on a sheet of paper where you indicate how many of each item you want, similar to a sushi restaurant. For anyone new to the dumpling scene, they have a menu with descriptions and photos of each item, so it makes it really easy to order.

Most of the plates come in portions that are shareable, so I would recommend trying a little bit of everything if you're there with a group. Family style worked really well for us since we all wanted to order almost everything on the menu.

I would highly recommend the Pork XiaoLongBao (steamed dumplings with a little soup in each), Sauteed String Beans with Garlic, Vegetable & Pork Wontons with Spicy Sauce, and Noodles with Sesame Sauce. YUM!

We also ordered drinks and I had what I think was called the Golden Emporer, it was an Old Fashioned type drink and was just as delicious.

Jedi was great to us and we all really enjoyed our dinner. The only reason I docked a star was because the bar was super backed up and we didn't receive our drinks until we were pretty much finished with dinner. But next time I'm in town, I'll definitely be back.</Text><pics>None<//pics><response>None<//response>< GmapID>

< Review>
Din Tai Fung makes me cry of happiness. I've been here twice and both times I think I went to heaven. Every bite is like a chorus of angels caressing your tongue. This is ambrosia. This is God's food. My girlfriend has dreams about the spicy chicken wontons. The soup xiao long bao is perfection. The memory of the taste of the chocolate xiao long bao haunts my tongue whenever i eat inferior sweets (read: all sweets). If you love yourself, go to din tai fung. This location has almost NO wait usually, which is unheard of. at the Glendale location, you can wait up to four hours, but the most I've waited here is about 20 minutes. The staff is always INCREDIBLE, friendly, knowledgeable, and helpful. No one there looks like they hate their job (it's probably because they're having lunch there, too). Anyway, self care is going to din tai fung. it has a Michelin star for a reason, and this is the best location in terms of wait time by far.<//Review>

< Review>
Great xiao long bao, sauteed kale, beef braised noodle soup, shu mai, pork chop and fried rice.  Din Tai Fung is more expensive than your typical dim sum restaurant but you are paying for the quality of the food ,exceptional service ( which is non existent in most Chinese resturants) and ambiance. If you despise an extensive wait time like I do,  go during off peak hours early lunch or early dinner.<//Review>

<user_name>Margaret Tsang</user_name>< Review>
It was 3:45pm on march 25, 2016 and we placed our 3 person table request at reception. After waited for 15 minutes and seeing they were seating 3 people tables arrived after us, we found out they did not even enter our names for table request on their system!

Ok, human error, but no apologies? After they found out their mistake, they were still seating 4 more small tables before us and it took them 5 more minutes before they seated us. When we got into the dinning area, their house was not busy and there were 4 other 3-ppl tables open. So they simply took their time to set our table even they knew they made the mistake and with no apologies.

After we got seated we gave our server Jane our order sheet right away. Great. 15 minutes later, we thought we will get our food to stuff my starving toddler. And we saw people who came in later already eating. Apparently she didn't enter our order into the system until 17 minutes after we handed her our order sheet.

Almost everything went wrong with our order. We asked for less salt in our veggie, and they ended up with no salt instead. We asked for half sugar in the Boba milk tea, and ended up with full sugar. We added a couple of dishes and it took them another 15 minutes for them to show up, of course our dear Jane forgot to enter the order again.

Food was good but very disappointed with their reception service today. We have been to this same location multiple times and was pretty good, until today, very disappointed. If it was rush hour, we would understand, but it was 4pm in the afternoon. Come on!<//Review>

< Review>
Food was OK, nothing to rave about. Service seemed very rushed. Prices are super high for what you get. I can get the same food that tastes much better in the SGV at a hole in the wall.

Came here for lunch with a friend recently, it's located inside the mall which is kind of irritating. I have to walk through a bunch of shops to get to the restaurant. The interior Decour is very nice, but that is also reflected in the high prices. We ordered the XLB obviously, and the garlic green beans to start. The garlic green beans actually tasted pretty good. However their signature XLB was super tiny, and very bland, didn't taste good at all. In addition they were lukewarm which means they have been sitting out for a while before being brought to the table.

Truthfully, I can get bigger, better tasting, better quality XLB at many different locations in the SGV for literally half of the price. I feel like this place is way too hyped up and not worth the price or the hassle.

Service was extremely rushed, it seems like they were really trying to get us out of there as soon as possible. Parking was a total nightmare near the mall. Even on a weekday at lunchtime.

I really don't like this place. Will not be returning!</Review>

<UserId.>117332549042307750756<//UserId.>< username>
K S< /username>
< Time>
1500330646982< /Time>
<rate>5</rate>< Review>
Pork XiaoLongBao soup dumplings:  Don't worry about the pronunciation, they give you a sheet to order from by quantifying the items you'd like and handing it to your server.  Pork filled dumplings with  warm broth.  Be careful!  Give time for dumplings to cool, eat in one bite because the broth will squirt out everywhere.  Perfect ratio of pork and dough with a delicious broth.   I can understand some reviewers critiquing the dumplings as "plain" but just dip in soy sauce and problem solved.

Shrimp and Pork Wontons:  This is the only reason for deduction.  The wonton dough was perfection, but the shrimp and Pork combination were not harmonious to the palate.   The design of the wonton, with the shrimp on top and pork at the bottom of dough,  just didn't mesh at all.  I would skip ordering this dish next time, but you never know until you try.

Vegetable and Pork Dumplings with Spicy Sauce:  Not even by my "white girl" terms is this spicy.  But the spicy/sweet sauce is divine.   I even smothered my other dumplings into that goodness, you may get looks, but do it!

Pear and Lychee Martini:  I am always blown away at restaurants that can craft exquisite cocktails to enjoy with their food.  The bartenders are very knowledgeful and really take the time to craft your drinks (rubbing orange peel on rim of glass and using fresh ingredients). Yes, the place does get packed but stand in line for the bar area if 21 and over to expedite your wait time.

The restaurant is huge but definitely gets filled quickly especially during peak hours of happy hour and weekends.  Received top service from everyone from the hostess, bartender,  and our server.  Clean, oh my goodness, so clean!

Price wise, I thought all of the items were reasonably priced.  I don't understand people that expect 5 star food on a 1 star budget.  I will be back without a doubt!<//Review>

2< /Rating>
<Text>I dined here this past Tuesday night with a party of 5, got a # a little before 6pm and was seated at 8pm. No problem, I knew there'd be a wait, I even ate a snack before heading to the mall. I love that DTF efficiently uses technology of texting you when it's time. However, I felt slightly cheated that upon checking in, I had to wait another 15 minutes before actually getting seated. What a tease!

I had their XLB pork, XLB crab/pork, seafood stir fry noodles, fried rice, spicy wontons, green beans, and veggie bun.

I was disappointed with the lack of soup inside the XLB and the pork was bland. The XLB crab/pork was actually more on the dry side.

Seafood stir fry noodles were bland and on the greasy side that lacked seafood. The fried rice was pretty tasty and not too oily as were their signature green beans. I think the spicy wontons were my favorite part of this meal. The sauce they use was so good, that I drizzled the sauce onto the stir fry noodles.

The pork bun and veggie bun were marked incorrectly. Green dot on top stood for veggie while the red for pork. After biting into this mistake, my friend and I traded since I ordered veggie and he ordered pork. The veggie bun itself was pretty good and filled with an abundance of minced green veggies. However, I've had stomach issues since after this meal and the only thing that I ate that no one else in my group ate was the veggie bun. That may be the culprit for my frequent restroom use.

Service was so-so, the server forgot a few items on the original print-out, but later remembered and added them. The pork and veggie buns were added later. He didn't check up on us as much as we'd liked and it was difficult to wave him down.

Since this DTF location just opened about 2 weeks ago, I think they need to have a pep talk with the cooks. I'm not impressed with this location compared to their Costa Mesa, Arcadia, and Glendale locations.</Text><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>
None</Resp>

(Translated by Google) Well worth the michellin star. This Taiwanese restaurant has been awarded a michellin star. In the middle of the largest shopping center in the United States, this restaurant has all kinds of dim sum, buns and other Taiwanese dishes. These dishes are very tasty and well worth going to. Some people may find it too expensive, but a dish costs between 5 and 25 dollars but on average about 10 dollars. The interior is very chic and certainly adds to the atmosphere. It is always busy in this restaurant and sometimes there is a queue. You can then draw a number and you will receive an email when there is a table. By the way, there is always a queue in L.A. The staff are nice and know almost everything about the menu. Our waitress knew it all and could recommend good dishes. The portions are not very large, but certainly filling and it is nice to combine different things. In short, this chain is a hit and anyone who likes good quality food will love this. Super!

(Original)
De michellin ster zeker waard. Dit Taiwanese restaurant is bekroont met een michellin ster. Midden in het grootste winkelcentrum van de Verenigde Staten staat dit restaurant wat allemaal soorten dim sum, buns en andere Taiwanese gerechten. Deze gerechten zijn erg lekker en zeker de moeite waard om naar toe te gaan. Sommige mensen zullen het misschien te duur vinden maar een gerecht kost tussen de 5 en 25 dollar maar gemiddeld zo'n 10 dollar. Het interieur is zeer shique en zeker een goede toevoeging aan de sfeer. Het is altijd druk in dit restaurant en soms is er een wachtrij. Je kan dan een nummertje trekken en je krijgt een e-mail als er een tafel is. Overigens is er in L.A. altijd een wachtrij. Het personeel is aardig en weet bijna alles van de kaart. Onze serveerster wist het allemaal en kon goede gerechten aanraden. De porties zijn niet heel groot maar zeker vullend en het is lekker om verschillende dingen te combineren.
